I mean when you really sit down and think about this amazing sport of MMA... The level of competition at the top is so insane! These guys are absolutely trained killers and we measure the success of a fighter on their ability to inflict bodily harm to their opponent with the ultimate goal being able to stop just before they do permanent damage to their opponent. Sure they are not actually going in their with guns & knives attempting to kill each other but what do you see every fighter (well 98% of them) do after they knock their opponent out unconscious... they always rain down a few hammer fists until the ref waves them off... So, yes they are actually trained to finish opponents and if left alone they would do serious harm if not deliver a fatal blow to the other fighter. It's such a fine line, I cannot believe in all the years this sport has not had a fatality on live tv. While it is rare, people do get killed in this sport... It just hasn't happened in a main, televised event yet and I pray it never does... It's far too early in the progression of MMA competition to understand what kind of long term damage they are doing to their bodies. When you see what it's done to them in boxing and the NFL, you would think the UFC would invest a little money into long term affects to possibly develope better protective equipment or preventative measures for the fighters but I guess for such an extremely violent sport like MMA... The fans want more blood, not more gear. Lol... Sry for long comment, when I heard Dustin say that he prays for a safe fight for both fighters before a fight because I know what I'm gonna be trying to do to him and he's gonna be trying to do the same thing to me.
